###DIALOGUE###Oh yeah, SNAPE.''
###DIALOGUE###``SNAPE?''
###DIALOGUE###``Yeah -- yer not still on abou' that, are yeh? 
###DIALOGUE###Look, SNAPE helped protect the Stone, SNAPE's not about ter steal it.''
HARRY knew RON and HERMIONE were thinking the same as HARRY was. 
If SNAPE had been in on protecting the Stone, it must have been easy to find out how the other teachers had guarded it. 
SNAPE probably knew everything -- except, it seemed, QUIRRELL's spell and how to get past Fluffy.
###DIALOGUE###``You're the only one who knows how to get past Fluffy. 
###DIALOGUE###aren't you, HAGRID?'' said HARRY anxiously. 
###DIALOGUE###``And you wouldn't tell anyone, would you? 
###DIALOGUE###Not even one of the teachers?''
###DIALOGUE###``Not a soul knows except me an' DUMBLEDORE,'' said HAGRID proudly.
###DIALOGUE###``Well, that's something,'' HARRY muttered to the others. 
###DIALOGUE###``HAGRID, can we have a window open? 
###DIALOGUE###I'm boiling.''
###DIALOGUE###``Can't, HARRY, sorry,'' said HAGRID. 
HARRY noticed HARRY glance at the fire. 
HARRY looked at it, too.
###DIALOGUE###``HAGRID -- what's that?''
But HARRY already knew what it was. 
In the very heart of the fire, underneath the kettle, was a huge, black egg.
###DIALOGUE###``Ah,'' said HAGRID, fiddling nervously with HARRY's beard, ``That's er...''
###DIALOGUE###``Where did you get it, HAGRID?'' said RON, crouching over the fire to get a closer look at the egg. 
###DIALOGUE###``It must've cost you a fortune.''
###DIALOGUE###``Won it,'' said HAGRID. 
###DIALOGUE###``Las' night. 
###DIALOGUE###I was down in the village havin' a few drinks an' got into a game o' cards with a stranger. 
###DIALOGUE###Think he was quite glad ter get rid of it, ter be honest.''
###DIALOGUE###``But what are you going to do with it when it's hatched?'' said HERMIONE.
###DIALOGUE###``Well, I've bin doin' some readin' , said HAGRID, pulling a large book from under his pillow. 
###DIALOGUE###``Got this outta the library -- Dragon Breeding for Pleasure and Profit -- it's a bit outta date, o' course, but it's all in here. 
Keep the egg in the fire, 'cause their mothers breathe on I em, see, an' when it hatches, feed it on a bucket o' brandy mixed with chicken blood every half hour. 
An' see here -- how ter recognize diff`rent eggs -- what I got there's a Norwegian Ridgeback. 
###DIALOGUE###They're rare, them.''
RON looked very pleased with himself, but HERMIONE didn't.
###DIALOGUE###``HAGRID, you live in a wooden house,'' HERMIONE said.
But HAGRID wasn't listening. 
RON was humming merrily as RON stoked the fire.
So now they had something else to worry about: what might happen to HAGRID if anyone found out RON was hiding an illegal dragon in RON's hut.
###DIALOGUE###``Wonder what it's like to have a peaceful life,'' RON sighed, as evening after evening they struggled through all the extra homework they were getting. 
HERMIONE had now started making study schedules for HARRY and RON, too. 
It was driving them nuts.
Then, one breakfast time, HEDWIG brought HARRY another note from HAGRID.
HARRY had written only two words: It's hatching.
RON wanted to skip Herbology and go straight down to the hut. 
HERMIONE wouldn't hear of it.
###DIALOGUE###``HERMIONE, how many times in our lives are we going to see a dragon hatching?''
###DIALOGUE###``We've got lessons, we'll get into trouble, and that's nothing to what HAGRID's going to be in when someone finds out what he's doing --''
###DIALOGUE###``Shut up!'' 
HARRY whispered.
MALFOY was only a few feet away and MALFOY had stopped dead to listen. 
How much had MALFOY heard? 
HARRY didn't like the look on MALFOY's face at all.
RON and HERMIONE argued all the way to Herbology and in the end, HERMIONE agreed to run down to HAGRID's with the other two during morning break. 
When the bell sounded from the castle at the end of their lesson, the three of them dropped their trowels at once and hurried through the grounds to the edge of the forest. 
HAGRID greeted them, looking flushed and excited.
###DIALOGUE###``It's nearly out.'' 
RON ushered them inside.
The egg was lying on the table. 
There were deep cracks in it. 
Something was moving inside; a funny clicking noise was coming from it.
They all drew their chairs up to the table and watched with bated breath.
All at once there was a scraping noise and the egg split open. 
The baby dragon flopped onto the table. 
It wasn't exactly pretty; HARRY thought it looked like a crumpled, black umbrella. 
Its spiny wings were huge compared to its skinny jet body, it had a long snout with wide nostrils, the stubs of horns and bulging, orange eyes.
It sneezed. 
A couple of sparks flew out of its snout.
###DIALOGUE###``Isn't he beautiful?'' 
HAGRID murmured. 
HARRY reached out a hand to stroke the dragon's head. 
It snapped at HARRY's fingers, showing pointed fangs.
###DIALOGUE###``Bless him, look, he knows his mommy!'' said HAGRID.
###DIALOGUE###``HAGRID,'' said HERMIONE, ``how fast do Norwegian Ridgebacks grow, exactly?''
HAGRID was about to answer when the color suddenly drained from HARRY's face -- HARRY leapt to HARRY's feet and ran to the window.
###DIALOGUE###``What's the matter?''
###DIALOGUE###``Someone was lookin' through the gap in the curtains -- it's a kid -- he's runnin' back up ter the school.''
HARRY bolted to the door and looked out. 
Even at a distance there was no mistaking HARRY.
MALFOY had seen the dragon.
Something about the smile lurking on MALFOY's face during the next week made HARRY, RON, and HERMIONE very nervous. 
They spent most of their free time in HAGRID's darkened hut, trying to reason with HARRY.
###DIALOGUE###``Just let him go,'' HARRY urged. 
###DIALOGUE###``Set him free.''
###DIALOGUE###``I can't,'' said HAGRID. 
###DIALOGUE###``He's too little. 
###DIALOGUE###He'd die.''
They looked at the dragon. 
It had grown three times in length in just a week. 
Smoke kept furling out of its nostrils. 
HAGRID hadn't been doing HARRY's gamekeeping duties because the dragon was keeping HARRY so busy. 
There were empty brandy bottles and chicken feathers all over the floor.
###DIALOGUE###``I've decided to call him NORBERT,'' said HAGRID, looking at the dragon with misty eyes. 
###DIALOGUE###``He really knows me now, watch. 
###DIALOGUE###NORBERT! 
###DIALOGUE###NORBERT! 
###DIALOGUE###Where's Mommy?''
###DIALOGUE###``HAGRID's lost HAGRID's marbles,'' RON muttered in HARRY's ear.
###DIALOGUE###``HAGRID,'' said HARRY loudly, ``give it two weeks and NORBERT's going to be as long as your house. 
###DIALOGUE###MALFOY could go to DUMBLEDORE at any moment.''
HAGRID bit HAGRID's lip.
###DIALOGUE###``I -- I know I can't keep NORBERT forever, but I can't jus' dump NORBERT, I can't.''
HARRY suddenly turned to RON. 
CHARLIE, HARRY said.
###DIALOGUE###``You're losing it, too,'' said RON. 
###DIALOGUE###``I'm RON, remember?''
###DIALOGUE###``No -- CHARLIE -- your brother, CHARLIE. 
###DIALOGUE###In Romania. 
###DIALOGUE###Studying dragons.
We could send NORBERT to CHARLIE. 
###DIALOGUE###CHARLIE can take care of NORBERT and then put NORBERT back in the wild!''
###DIALOGUE###``Brilliant!'' said RON. 
###DIALOGUE###``How about it, HAGRID?''
And in the end, HAGRID agreed that they could send -an owl to CHARLIE to ask CHARLIE.
The following week dragged by. 
Wednesday night found HERMIONE and HARRY sitting alone in the common room, long after everyone else had gone to bed. 
The clock on the wall had just chimed midnight when the portrait hole burst open. 
RON appeared out of nowhere as RON pulled off HARRY's invisibility cloak. 
HARRY had been down at HAGRID's hut, helping HARRY feed NORBERT, who was now eating dead rats by the crate.
###DIALOGUE###``It bit me!'' 
NORBERT said, showing them NORBERT's hand, which was wrapped in a bloody handkerchief. 
###DIALOGUE###``I'm not going to be able to hold a quill for a week. 
###DIALOGUE###I tell you, that dragon's the most horrible animal I've ever met, but the way HAGRID goes on about it, you'd think it was a fluffy little bunny rabbit. 
###DIALOGUE###When it bit me he told me off for frightening it. 
###DIALOGUE###And when I left, he was singing it a lullaby.''
There was a tap on the dark window.
###DIALOGUE###``It's Hedwig!'' said HARRY, hurrying to let RON in. 
###DIALOGUE###``She'll have CHARLIE's answer!''
The three of them put their heads together to read the note.
Dear RON,
How are you? 
Thanks for the letter -- I'd be glad to take the Norwegian Ridgeback, but it won't be easy getting him here. 
I think the best thing will be to send him over with some friends of mine who are coming to visit me next week. 
Trouble is, they mustn't be seen carrying an illegal dragon.
Could you get the Ridgeback up the tallest tower at midnight on Saturday? 
They can meet you there and take him away while it's still dark.
Send me an answer as soon as possible.
Love,
CHARLIE
They looked at one another.
###DIALOGUE###``We've got the invisibility cloak,'' said HARRY. 
###DIALOGUE###``It shouldn't be too difficult -- I think the cloaks big enough to cover two of us and NORBERT.''
It was a mark of how bad the last week had been that the other two agreed with HARRY. 
Anything to get rid of NORBERT -- and MALFOY.
There was a hitch. 
By the next morning, RON's bitten hand had swollen to twice its usual size. 
RON didn't know whether it was safe to go to Madam Pomfrey -- would she recognize a dragon bite? 
By the afternoon, though, RON had no choice. 
The cut had turned a nasty shade of green. 
It looked as if NORBERT's fangs were poisonous.
HARRY and HERMIONE rushed up to the hospital wing at the end of the day to find RON in a terrible state in bed.
###DIALOGUE###``It's not just my hand,'' RON whispered, ``although that feels like it's about to fall off. 
###DIALOGUE###MALFOY told POMFREY MALFOY wanted to borrow one of my books so MALFOY could come and have a good laugh at me. 
###DIALOGUE###MALFOY kept threatening to tell POMFREY's what really bit me -- I've told POMFREY's it was a dog, but I don't think POMFREY believes me -I shouldn't have hit MALFOY at the Quidditch match, that's why MALFOY's doing this.''
HARRY and HERMIONE tried to calm RON down.
###DIALOGUE###``It'll all be over at midnight on Saturday,'' said HERMIONE, but this didn't soothe RON at all. 
On the contrary, RON sat bolt upright and broke into a sweat.
###DIALOGUE###``Midnight on Saturday!'' 
RON said in a hoarse voice. 
###DIALOGUE###``Oh no oh no -- I've just remembered -- CHARLIE's letter was in that book MALFOY took, MALFOY's going to know we're getting rid of NORBERT.''
HARRY and HERMIONE didn't get a chance to answer. 
POMFREY came over at that moment and made them leave, saying RON needed sleep.
###DIALOGUE###``It's too late to change the plan now,'' HARRY told HERMIONE. 
###DIALOGUE###``We haven't got time to send CHARLIE another owl, and this could be our only chance to get rid of NORBERT. 
###DIALOGUE###We'll have to risk it. 
###DIALOGUE###And we have got the invisibility cloak, MALFOY doesn't know about that.''
They found FANG, the boarhound, sitting outside with a bandaged tail when they went to tell HAGRID, who opened a window to talk to them.
###DIALOGUE###``I won't let you in,'' HARRY puffed. 
###DIALOGUE###``NORBERT's at a tricky stage -- nothin' I can't handle.''
When they told HARRY about CHARLIE's letter, CHARLIE's eyes filled with tears, although that might have been because NORBERT had just bitten NORBERT on the leg.
###DIALOGUE###``Aargh! 
###DIALOGUE###It's all right, NORBERT only got my boot -- jus' playin' -- NORBERT's only a baby, after all.''
The baby banged its tail on the wall, making the windows rattle. 
HARRY and HERMIONE walked back to the castle feeling Saturday couldn't come quickly enough.
They would have felt sorry for HAGRID when the time came for HARRY to say good-bye to NORBERT if they hadn't been so worried about what they had to do. 
It was a very dark, cloudy night, and they were a bit late arriving at HAGRID's hut because they'd had to wait for Peeves to get out of their way in the entrance hall, where NORBERT'd been playing tennis against the wall. 
HAGRID had NORBERT packed and ready in a large crate.
###DIALOGUE###``NORBERT's got lots o' rats an' some brandy fer the journey,'' said HAGRID in a muffled voice. 
###DIALOGUE###``An' I've packed NORBERT's teddy bear in case NORBERT gets lonely.''
From inside the crate came ripping noises that sounded to HARRY as though the teddy was having HARRY's head torn off.
###DIALOGUE###``Bye-bye, NORBERT!'' 
HAGRID sobbed, as HARRY and HERMIONE covered the crate with the invisibility cloak and stepped underneath it themselves.
###DIALOGUE###``Mommy will never forget you!''
How they managed to get the crate back up to the castle, they never knew. 
Midnight ticked nearer as they heaved NORBERT up the marble staircase in the entrance hall and along the dark corridors. 
UP another staircase, then another -- even one of HARRY's shortcuts didn't make the work much easier.
###DIALOGUE###``Nearly there!'' 
HARRY panted as they reached the corridor beneath the tallest tower.
Then a sudden movement ahead of them made them almost drop the crate.
Forgetting that they were already invisible, they shrank into the shadows, staring at the dark outlines of two people grappling with each other ten feet away. 
A lamp flared.
MCGONAGALL, in a tartan bathrobe and a hair net, had MALFOY by the ear.
###DIALOGUE###``Detention!'' she shouted. 
###DIALOGUE###``And twenty points from SLYTHERIN! 
###DIALOGUE###Wandering around in the middle of the night, how dare you --''
###DIALOGUE###``You don't understand, Professor. 
###DIALOGUE###HARRY 's coming -- HARRY's got a dragon!''
###DIALOGUE###``What utter rubbish! 
###DIALOGUE###How dare you tell such lies! 
###DIALOGUE###Come on -- I shall see SNAPE about you, MALFOY!''
The steep spiral staircase up to the top of the tower seemed the easiest thing in the world after that. 
Not until they'd stepped out into the cold night air did they throw off the cloak, glad to be able to breathe properly again. 
HERMIONE did a sort of jig.
###DIALOGUE###``MALFOY's got detention! 
###DIALOGUE###I could sing!''
###DIALOGUE###``Don't,'' HARRY advised HERMIONE.
Chuckling about MALFOY, they waited, NORBERT thrashing about in NORBERT's crate. 
About ten minutes later, four broomsticks came swooping down out of the darkness.
CHARLIE's friends were a cheery lot. 
They showed HARRY and HERMIONE the harness they'd rigged up, so they could suspend NORBERT between them.
They all helped buckle NORBERT safely into it and then HARRY and HERMIONE shook hands with the others and thanked them very much.
At last, NORBERT was going... going... gone.
They slipped back down the spiral staircase, their hearts as light as their hands, now that NORBERT was off them. 
No more dragon -- MALFOY in detention -- what could spoil their happiness? 
The answer to that was waiting at the foot of the stairs. 
As they stepped into the corridor, FILCH's face loomed suddenly out of the darkness.
###DIALOGUE###``Well, well, well,'' he whispered, ``we are in trouble.''
They'd left the invisibility cloak on top of the tower.
CHAPTER FIFTEEN
THE FORIBIDDEN FOREST
Things couldn't have been worse.
FILCH took them down to MCGONAGALL's study on the first floor, where they sat and waited without saying a word to each other. 
HERMIONE was trembling. 
Excuses, alibis, and wild cover- up stories chased each other around HARRY's brain, each more feeble than the last. 
HARRY couldn't see how they were going to get out of trouble this time. 
They were cornered. 
How could they have been so stupid as to forget the cloak? 
There was no reason on earth that MCGONAGALL would accept for their being out of bed and creeping around the school in the dead of night, let alone being up the tallest astRONomy tower, which was out-of-bounds except for classes. 
Add NORBERT and the invisibility cloak, and they might as well be packing their bags already.
Had HARRY thought that things couldn't have been worse? 
He was wrong.
When MCGONAGALL appeared, she was leading NEVILLE.
###DIALOGUE###``HARRY!'' 
NEVILLE burst Out, the moment NEVILLE saw the other two. 
###DIALOGUE###``I was trying to find you to warn you, I heard MALFOY saying MALFOY was going to catch you, MALFOY said you had a drag --''
HARRY shook HARRY's head violently to shut NEVILLE up, but MCGONAGALL had seen. 
She looked more likely to breathe fire than NORBERT as she towered over the three of them.
###DIALOGUE###``I would never have believed it of any of you. 
###DIALOGUE###FILCH says you were up in the astRONomy tower. 
###DIALOGUE###It's one o'clock in the morning. 
###DIALOGUE###Explain yourselves.''
It was the first time HERMIONE had ever failed to answer a teacher's question. 
HERMIONE was staring at HERMIONE's slippers, as still as a statue.
###DIALOGUE###``I think I've got a good idea of what's been going on,'' said MCGONAGALL. 
###DIALOGUE###``It doesn't take a genius to work it out. 
###DIALOGUE###You fed MALFOY some cock-and-bull story about a dragon, trying to get MALFOY out of bed and into trouble. 
###DIALOGUE###I've already caught MALFOY. 
###DIALOGUE###I suppose you think it's funny that NEVILLE here heard the story and believed it, too?''
HARRY caught NEVILLE's eye and tried to tell HARRY without words that this wasn't true, because NEVILLE was looking stunned and hurt. 
Poor, blundering NEVILLE -- HARRY knew what it must have cost HARRY to try and find them in the dark, to warn them.
###DIALOGUE###``I'm disgusted,'' said MCGONAGALL. 
###DIALOGUE###``Four students out of bed in one night! 
###DIALOGUE###I've never heard of such a thing before! 
###DIALOGUE###You, HERMIONE , I thought you had more sense. 
###DIALOGUE###As for you, HARRY , I thought GRYFFINDOR meant more to you than this. 
###DIALOGUE###All three of you will receive detentions -- yes, you too, Mr. Longbottom, nothing gives you the right to walk around school at night, especially these days, it's very dangerous -- and fifty points will be taken from GRYFFINDOR.''
###DIALOGUE###``Fifty?'' 
HARRY gasped -- they would lose the lead, the lead HARRY'd won in the last Quidditch match.
###DIALOGUE###``Fifty points each,'' said MCGONAGALL, breathing heavily through HERMIONE's long, pointed nose.
###DIALOGUE###``Professor -- please ``You can't --''
###DIALOGUE###``Don't tell me what I can and can't do, HARRY. 
###DIALOGUE###Now get back to bed, all of you. 
###DIALOGUE###I've never been more ashamed of GRYFFINDOR students.''
A hundred and fifty points lost. 
That put GRYFFINDOR in last place. 
In one night, they'd ruined any chance GRYFFINDOR had had for the house cup. 
HARRY felt as though the bottom had dropped out of HARRY's stomach. 
How could they ever make up for this? 
HARRY didn't sleep all night. 
HARRY could hear NEVILLE sobbing into NEVILLE's pillow for what seemed like hours. 
HARRY couldn't think of anything to say to comfort HARRY. 
HARRY knew NEVILLE, like himself, was dreading the dawn. 
What would happen when the rest of GRYFFINDOR found out what they'd done? 
At first, GRYFFINDORS passing the giant hourglasses that recorded the house points the next day thought there'd been a mistake. 
How could they suddenly have a hundred and fifty points fewer than yesterday? 
And then the story started to spread: HARRY , the famous HARRY , their hero of two Quidditch matches, had lo st them all those points, HARRY and a couple of other stupid first years.
From being one of the most popular and admired people at the school, HARRY was suddenly the most hated. 
Even RAVENCLAWS and HUFFLEPUFFS turned on HARRY, because everyone had been longing to see SLYTHERIN lose the house cup. 
Everywhere HARRY went, people pointed and didn't trouble to lower their voices as they insulted HARRY. 
###DIALOGUE###SLYTHERINS, on the other hand, clapped as HARRY walked past them, whistling and cheering, ``Thanks HARRY, we owe you one!''
Only RON stood by RON.
###DIALOGUE###``They'll all forget this in a few weeks. 
###DIALOGUE###FRED and GEORGE have lost loads of points in all the time they've been here, and people still like them.''
###DIALOGUE###``They've never lost a hundred and fifty points in one go, though, have they?'' said HARRY miserably.
###DIALOGUE###``Well -- no,'' RON admitted.
It was a bit late to repair the damage, but HARRY swore to himself not to meddle in things that weren't HARRY's business from now on. 
HARRY'd had it with sneaking around and spying. 
HARRY felt so ashamed of himself that HARRY went to WOOD and offered to resign from the Quidditch team.
###DIALOGUE###``Resign?'' 
WOOD thundered. 
###DIALOGUE###``What good'll that do? 
###DIALOGUE###How are we going to get any points back if we can't win at Quidditch?''
But even Quidditch had lost its fun. 
###DIALOGUE###The rest of the team wouldn't speak to HARRY during practice, and if they had to speak about HARRY, they called HARRY ``the Seeker.''
HERMIONE and NEVILLE were suffering, too. 
They didn't have as bad a time as HARRY, because they weren't as well-known, but nobody would speak to them, either. 
HERMIONE had stopped drawing attention to herself in class, keeping HERMIONE's head down and working in silence.
HARRY was almost glad that the exams weren't far away. 
All the studying HARRY had to do kept HARRY's mind off HARRY's misery. 
HARRY, RON, and HERMIONE kept to themselves, working late into the night, trying to remember the ingredients in complicated potions, learn charms and spells by heart, memorize the dates of magical discoveries and goblin rebellions...
Then, about a week before the exams were due to start, HARRY's new resolution not to interfere in anything that didn't concern HARRY was put to an unexpected test. 
Walking back from the library on HARRY's own one afternoon, HARRY heard somebody whimpering from a classroom up ahead. 
As HARRY drew closer, HARRY heard QUIRRELL's voice.
###DIALOGUE###``No -- no -- not again, please --''
It sounded as though someone was threatening HARRY. 
HARRY moved closer.
###DIALOGUE###``All right -- all right --'' HARRY heard QUIRRELL sob.
Next second, QUIRRELL came hurrying out of the classroom straightening HARRY's turban. 
HARRY was pale and looked as though HARRY was about to cry. 
HARRY strode out of sight; HARRY didn't think QUIRRELL had even noticed HARRY.
HARRY waited until QUIRRELL's footsteps had disappeared, then peered into the classroom. 
It was empty, but a door stood ajar at the other end.
HARRY was halfway toward it before HARRY remembered what HARRY'd promised himself about not meddling.
All the same, HARRY'd have gambled twelve Sorcerer's Stones that SNAPE had just left the room, and from what HARRY had just heard, SNAPE would be walking with a new spring in HARRY's step -- QUIRRELL seemed to have given in at last.
HARRY went back to the library, where HERMIONE was testing RON on AstRONomy. 
HARRY told them what HARRY'd heard.
###DIALOGUE###``SNAPE's done it, then!'' said RON. 
###DIALOGUE###``If QUIRRELL's told SNAPE how to break SNAPE's Anti-Dark Force spell --''
###DIALOGUE###``There's still Fluffy, though,'' said HERMIONE.
###DIALOGUE###``Maybe SNAPE's found out how to get past SNAPE without asking HAGRID,'' said RON, looking up at the thousands of books surrounding them. 
###DIALOGUE###``I bet there's a book somewhere in here telling you how to get past a giant three-headed dog. 
###DIALOGUE###So what do we do, HARRY?''
The light of adventure was kindling again in RON's eyes, but HERMIONE answered before HARRY could.
###DIALOGUE###``Go to DUMBLEDORE. 
###DIALOGUE###That's what we should have done ages ago. 
###DIALOGUE###If we try anything ourselves we'll be thrown out for sure.''
###DIALOGUE###``But we've got no proof!'' said HARRY. 
###DIALOGUE###``QUIRRELL's too scared to back us up. 
###DIALOGUE###SNAPE's only got to say SNAPE doesn't know how the troll got in at Halloween and that SNAPE was nowhere near the third floor -- who do you think they'll believe, SNAPE or us? 
###DIALOGUE###It's not exactly a secret we hate SNAPE, DUMBLEDORE'll think we made it up to get DUMBLEDORE sacked. 
###DIALOGUE###FILCH wouldn't help us if DUMBLEDORE's life depended on it, DUMBLEDORE's too friendly with SNAPE, and the more students get thrown out, the better, SNAPE'll think. 
###DIALOGUE###And don't forget, we're not supposed to know about the Stone or Fluffy. 
###DIALOGUE###That'll take a lot of explaining.''
HERMIONE looked convinced, but RON didn't.
###DIALOGUE###``If we just do a bit of poking around --''
###DIALOGUE###``No,'' said HARRY flatly, ``we've done enough poking around.''
HARRY pulled a map of Jupiter toward HARRY and started to learn the names of its moons.
The following morning, notes were delivered to HARRY, HERMIONE, and NEVILLE at the breakfast table. 
They were all the same: Your detention will take place at eleven o'clock tonight. 
Meet FILCH in the entrance hall.
Professor McGonagall HARRY had forgotten they still had detentions to do in the furor over the points they'd lost. 
He half expected HERMIONE to complain that this was a whole night of studying lost, but HERMIONE didn't say a word. 
Like HARRY, HERMIONE felt they deserved what they'd got.
At eleven o'clock that night, they said good-bye to RON in the common room and went down to the entrance hall with NEVILLE. 
FILCH was already there -- and so was MALFOY. 
HARRY had also forgotten that MALFOY had gotten a detention, too.
###DIALOGUE###``Follow me,'' said FILCH, lighting a lamp and leading them outside.
###DIALOGUE###I bet you'll think twice about breaking a school rule again, won't you, eh?'' 
###DIALOGUE###HARRY said, leering at them. 
###DIALOGUE###``Oh yes... hard work and pain are the best teachers if you ask me... It's just a pity they let the old punishments die out... hang you by your wrists from the ceiling for a few days, I've got the chains still in my office, keep 'em well oiled in case they're ever needed... Right, off we go, and don't think of running off, now, it'll be worse for you if you do.''
They marched off across the dark grounds. 
NEVILLE kept sniffing. 
HARRY wondered what their punishment was going to be. 
It must be something really horrible, or FILCH wouldn't be sounding so delighted.
The moon was bright, but clouds scudding across it kept throwing them into darkness. 
Ahead, HARRY could see the lighted windows of HAGRID's hut. 
Then they heard a distant shout.
###DIALOGUE###``Is that you, FILCH? 
###DIALOGUE###Hurry up, I want ter get started.''
HARRY's heart rose; if they were going to be working with HAGRID it wouldn't be so bad. 
###DIALOGUE###HARRY's relief must have showed in HARRY's -face, because FILCH said, ``I suppose you think you'll be enjoying yourself with that oaf? 
###DIALOGUE###Well, think again, boy -- it's into the forest you're going and I'm much mistaken if you'll all come out in one piece.''
At this, NEVILLE let out a little moan, and MALFOY stopped dead in MALFOY's tracks.
###DIALOGUE###``The forest?'' 
MALFOY repeated, and MALFOY didn't sound quite as cool as usual.
###DIALOGUE###``We can't go in there at night -- there's all sorts of things in there -- werewolves, I heard.''
NEVILLE clutched the sleeve of HARRY's robe and made a choking noise.
###DIALOGUE###``That's your problem, isn't it?'' said FILCH, HARRY's voice cracking with glee. 
###DIALOGUE###``Should've thought of them werewolves before you got in trouble, shouldn't you?''
HAGRID came striding toward them out of the dark, FANG at FANG's heel. 
FANG was carrying FANG's large crossbow, and a quiver of arrows hung over FANG's shoulder.
###DIALOGUE###``Abou' time,'' FANG said. 
###DIALOGUE###``I bin waitin' fer half an hour already. 
###DIALOGUE###All right, HARRY, HERMIONE?''
###DIALOGUE###``I shouldn't be too friendly to them, HAGRID,'' said FILCH coldly, they're here to be punished, after all.''
###DIALOGUE###``That's why yer late, is it?'' said HAGRID, frowning at FILCH. 
###DIALOGUE###``Bin lecturin' them, eh? 
###DIALOGUE###`Snot your place ter do that. 
###DIALOGUE###Yeh've done yer bit, I'll take over from here.''
###DIALOGUE###``I'll be back at dawn,'' said FILCH, ``for what's left of them,'' FANG added nastily, and FANG turned and started back toward the castle, FANG's lamp bobbing away in the darkness.
MALFOY now turned to HAGRID.
###DIALOGUE###``I'm not going in that forest, HARRY said, and HARRY was pleased to hear the note of panic in HARRY's voice.
###DIALOGUE###``Yeh are if yeh want ter stay at HOGWARTS,'' said HAGRID fiercely.
###DIALOGUE###``Yeh've done wrong an' now yehve got ter pay fer it.''
###DIALOGUE###``But this is servant stuff, it's not for students to do. 
###DIALOGUE###I thought we'd be copying lines or something, if my father knew I was doing this, he'd tell yer that's how it is at HOGWARTS,'' HAGRID growled. 
###DIALOGUE###``Copyin' lines! 
###DIALOGUE###What good's that ter anyone? 
###DIALOGUE###Yeh'll do summat useful or Yeh'll get out.
If yeh think yer father'd rather you were expelled, then get back off ter the castle an' pack. 
###DIALOGUE###Go on''' MALFOY didn't move. 
###DIALOGUE###He looked at HAGRID furiously, but then dropped his gaze.
###DIALOGUE###``Right then,'' said HAGRID, ``now, listen carefully, 'cause it's dangerous what we're gonna do tonight, an' I don' want no one takin' risks. 
###DIALOGUE###Follow me over here a moment.''
He led them to the very edge of the forest. 
Holding his lamp up high, he pointed down a narrow, winding earth track that disappeared into the thick black trees. 
A light breeze lifted their hair as they looked into the forest.
###DIALOGUE###``Look there,'' said HAGRID, ``see that stuff shinin' on the ground? 
###DIALOGUE###Silvery stuff? 
###DIALOGUE###That's unicorn blood. 
###DIALOGUE###There's a unicorn in there bin hurt badly by summat. 
###DIALOGUE###This is the second time in a week. 
###DIALOGUE###I found one dead last Wednesday. 
###DIALOGUE###We're gonna try an' find the poor thing. 
###DIALOGUE###We might have ter put it out of its misery.''
###DIALOGUE###``And what if whatever hurt the unicorn finds us first?'' said MALFOY, unable to keep the fear out of MALFOY's voice.
###DIALOGUE###``There's nothin' that lives in the forest that'll hurt yeh if yer with me or FANG,'' said HAGRID. 
###DIALOGUE###``An' keep ter the path. 
###DIALOGUE###Right, now, we're gonna split inter two parties an' follow the trail in diff`rent directions. 
###DIALOGUE###There's blood all over the place, it must've bin staggerin' around since last night at least.''
###DIALOGUE###``I want Fang,'' said MALFOY quickly, looking at FANG's long teeth.
###DIALOGUE###``All right, but I warn yeh, he's a coward,'' said HAGRID. '' 
###DIALOGUE###So me, HARRY, an' HERMIONE'll go one way an' Draco, NEVILLE, an' Fang'll go the other.
Now, if any of us finds the unicorn, we'll send up green sparks, right? 
###DIALOGUE###Get yer wands out an' practice now -- that's it -- an' if anyone gets in trouble, send up red sparks, an' we'll all come an' find yeh -- so, be careful -- let's go.''
The forest was black and silent. 
A little way into it they reached a fork in the earth path, and HARRY, HERMIONE, and HAGRID took the left path while MALFOY, NEVILLE, and FANG took the right.
They walked in silence, their eyes on the ground. 
Every now and then a ray of moonlight through the branches above lit a spot of silver-blue blood on the fallen leaves.
HARRY saw that HAGRID looked very worried.
###DIALOGUE###``Could a werewolf be killing the unicorns?'' 
HARRY asked.
###DIALOGUE###``Not fast enough,'' said HAGRID. 
###DIALOGUE###``It's not easy ter catch a unicorn, they're powerful magic creatures. 
###DIALOGUE###I never knew one ter be hurt before.''
They walked past a mossy tree stump. 
HARRY could hear running water; there must be a stream somewhere close by. 
There were still spots of unicorn blood here and there along the winding path.
###DIALOGUE###``You all right, HERMIONE?'' 
HAGRID whispered. 
###DIALOGUE###``Don' worry, it can't've gone far if it's this badly hurt, an' then we'll be able ter -- GET BEHIND THAT TREE!''
HAGRID seized HARRY and HERMIONE and hoisted them off the path behind a towering oak. 
HARRY pulled out an arrow and fitted it into HARRY's crossbow, raising it, ready to fire. 
The three of them listened. 
Something was slithering over dead leaves nearby: it sounded like a cloak trailing along the ground. 
HAGRID was squinting up the dark path, but after a few seconds, the sound faded away.
###DIALOGUE###``I knew it, '' HARRY murmured. 
###DIALOGUE###``There's summat in here that shouldn' be.''
###DIALOGUE###``A werewolf?'' 
HARRY suggested.
###DIALOGUE###``That wasn' no werewolf an' it wasn' no unicorn, neither,'' said HAGRID grimly. 
###DIALOGUE###``Right, follow me, but careful, now.''
They walked more slowly, ears straining for the faintest sound.
Suddenly, in a clearing ahead, something definitely moved.
###DIALOGUE###``Who's there?'' 
HAGRID called. 
###DIALOGUE###``Show yerself -- I'm armed!''
And into the clearing came -- was it a man, or a horse? 
To the waist, a man, with red hair and beard, but below that was a horse's gleaming chestnut body with a long, reddish tail. 
HARRY and HERMIONE's jaws dropped.
###DIALOGUE###``Oh, it's you, RONAN,'' said HAGRID in relief. 
###DIALOGUE###``How are yeh?''
HARRY walked forward and shook the centaur's hand.
###DIALOGUE###``Good evening to you, HAGRID,'' said RONAN. 
RONAN had a deep, sorrowful voice. 
###DIALOGUE###``Were you going to shoot me?''
###DIALOGUE###``Can't be too careful, RONAN,'' said HAGRID, patting RONAN's crossbow.
###DIALOGUE###``There's summat bad loose in this forest. 
###DIALOGUE###This is HARRY an' HERMIONE , by the way. 
###DIALOGUE###Students up at the school. 
###DIALOGUE###An' this is RONAN, you two. 
###DIALOGUE###RONAN's a centaur.-RRB--RRB- 
###DIALOGUE###``We'd noticed,'' said HERMIONE faintly.
###DIALOGUE###``Good evening,'' said RONAN. 
###DIALOGUE###``Students, are you? 
###DIALOGUE###And do you learn much, up at the school?''
###DIALOGUE###``Erm --''
###DIALOGUE###``A bit,'' said HERMIONE timidly.
###DIALOGUE###``A bit. 
###DIALOGUE###Well, that's something.'' 
RONAN sighed. 
RONAN flung back RONAN's head and stared at the sky. 
###DIALOGUE###``Mars is bright tonight.''
###DIALOGUE###``Yeah,'' said HAGRID, glancing up, too. 
###DIALOGUE###``Listen, I'm glad we've run inter yeh, RONAN, 'cause there's a unicorn bin hurt -- you seen anythin'?''
RONAN didn't answer immediately. 
RONAN stared unblinkingly upward, then sighed again.
###DIALOGUE###``Always the innocent are the first victims,'' RONAN said. 
###DIALOGUE###``So it has been for ages past, so it is now.''
###DIALOGUE###``Yeah,'' said HAGRID, ``but have yeh seen anythin', RONAN? 
###DIALOGUE###Anythin' unusual?''
###DIALOGUE###``Mars is bright tonight,'' RONAN repeated, while HAGRID watched RONAN impatiently. 
###DIALOGUE###``Unusually bright.''
###DIALOGUE###``Yeah, but I was meanin' anythin' unusual a bit nearer home, said HAGRID. 
###DIALOGUE###``So yeh haven't noticed anythin' strange?''
Yet again, RONAN took a while to answer. 
###DIALOGUE###At last, RONAN said, ``The forest hides many secrets.''
A movement in the trees behind RONAN made HAGRID raise RONAN's bow again, but it was only a second centaur, black-haired and -bodied and wilder-looking than RONAN.
###DIALOGUE###``Hullo, BANE,'' said HAGRID. 
###DIALOGUE###``All right?''
###DIALOGUE###``Good evening, HAGRID, I hope you are well?''
###DIALOGUE###``Well enough. 
###DIALOGUE###Look, I've jus' bin askin' RONAN, you seen anythin' odd in here lately? 
###DIALOGUE###There's a unicorn bin injured -- would yeh know anythin' about it?''
BANE walked over to stand next to RONAN. 
RONAN looked skyward. 
###DIALOGUE###``Mars is bright tonight,'' RONAN said simply.
###DIALOGUE###``We've heard,'' said HAGRID grumpily. 
###DIALOGUE###``Well, if either of you do see anythin', let me know, won't yeh? 
###DIALOGUE###We'll be off, then.''
HARRY and HERMIONE followed HARRY out of the clearing, staring over their shoulders at RONAN and BANE until the trees blocked their view.
###DIALOGUE###``Never,'' said HAGRID irritably, ``try an' get a straight answer out of a centaur. 
###DIALOGUE###Ruddy stargazers. 
###DIALOGUE###Not interested in anythin' closer'n the moon.''
###DIALOGUE###``Are there many of them in here?'' asked HERMIONE.
###DIALOGUE###``Oh, a fair few... Keep themselves to themselves mostly, but they're good enough about turnin' up if ever I want a word. 
###DIALOGUE###They're deep, mind, centaurs... they know things... jus' don' let on much.''
###DIALOGUE###``D'you think that was a centaur we heard earlier?'' said HARRY.
###DIALOGUE###``Did that sound like hooves to you? 
###DIALOGUE###Nah, if yeh ask me, that was what's bin killin' the unicorns -- never heard anythin' like it before.''
They walked on through the dense, dark trees. 
HARRY kept looking nervously over HARRY's shoulder. 
HARRY had the nasty feeling they were being watched. 
HARRY was very glad they had HAGRID and HARRY's crossbow with them.
They had just passed a bend in the path when HERMIONE grabbed HAGRID's arm.
###DIALOGUE###``HAGRID! 
###DIALOGUE###Look! 
###DIALOGUE###Red sparks, the others are in trouble!''
###DIALOGUE###``You two wait here!'' 
HAGRID shouted. 
###DIALOGUE###``Stay on the path, I'll come back for yeh!''
They heard HARRY crashing away through the undergrowth and stood looking at each other, very scared, until they couldn't hear anything but the rustling of leaves around them.
###DIALOGUE###``You don't think they've been hurt, do you?'' whispered HERMIONE.
###DIALOGUE###``I don't care if MALFOY has, but if something's got NEVILLE... it's our fault NEVILLE's here in the first place.''
The minutes dragged by. 
Their ears seemed sharper than usual. 
HARRY's seemed to be picking up every sigh of the wind, every cracking twig.
What was going on? 
Where were the others? 
At last, a great crunching noise announced HAGRID's return. 
MALFOY, NEVILLE, and FANG were with FANG. 
HAGRID was fuming. 
MALFOY, it seemed, had sneaked up behind NEVILLE and grabbed NEVILLE as a joke. 
NEVILLE had panicked and sent up the sparks.
###DIALOGUE###``We'll be lucky ter catch anythin' now, with the racket you two were makin'. 
###DIALOGUE###Right, we're changin' groups -- NEVILLE, you stay with me an' HERMIONE, HARRY, you go with FANG an' this idiot. 
###DIALOGUE###I'm sorry,'' HAGRID added in a whisper to HARRY, ``but FANG'll have a harder time frightenin' you, an' we've gotta get this done.''
So HARRY set off into the heart of the forest with MALFOY and FANG. 
They walked for nearly half an hour, deeper and deeper into the forest, until the path became almost impossible to follow because the trees were so thick. 
HARRY thought the blood seemed to be getting thicker. 
There were splashes on the roots of a tree, as though the poor creature had been thrashing around in pain close by. 
HARRY could see a clearing ahead, through the tangled branches of an ancient oak.
###DIALOGUE###``Look --'' HARRY murmured, holding out HARRY's arm to stop MALFOY.
Something bright white was gleaming on the ground. 
They inched closer.
It was the unicorn all right, and it was dead. 
HARRY had never seen anything so beautiful and sad. 
Its long, slender legs were stuck out at odd angles where it had fallen and its mane was spread pearly-white on the dark leaves.
HARRY had taken one step toward it when a slithering sound made HARRY freeze where HARRY stood. 
A bush on the edge of the clearing quivered...
Then, out of the shadows, a hooded figure came crawling across the ground like some stalking beast. 
HARRY, MALFOY, and FANG stood transfixed. 
The cloaked figure reached the unicorn, lowered its head over the wound in the animal's side, and began to drink its blood.
###DIALOGUE###``AAAAAAAAAARGH!''
MALFOY let out a terrible scream and bolted -- so did FANG. 
The hooded figure raised its head and looked right at HARRY -- unicorn blood was dribbling down its front. 
It got to its feet and came swiftly toward HARRY -- HARRY couldn't move for fear.
Then a pain like HARRY'd never felt before pierced HARRY's head; it was as though HARRY's scar were on fire. 
Half blinded, HARRY staggered backward. 
HARRY heard hooves behind HARRY, galloping, and something jumped clean over HARRY, charging at the figure.
The pain in HARRY's head was so bad HARRY fell to HARRY's knees. 
It took a minute or two to pass. 
When HARRY looked up, the figure had gone. 
A centaur was standing over HARRY, not RONAN or BANE; this one looked younger; RONAN had white-blond hair and a palomino body.
###DIALOGUE###``Are you all right?'' said the centaur, pulling HARRY to HARRY's feet.
###DIALOGUE###``Yes -- thank you -- what was that?''
The centaur didn't answer. 
HARRY had astonishingly blue eyes, like pale sapphires. 
HARRY looked carefully at HARRY, HARRY's eyes lingering on the scar that stood out, livid, on HARRY's forehead.
###DIALOGUE###``You are the HARRY boy,'' HARRY said. 
###DIALOGUE###``You had better get back to HAGRID.
The forest is not safe at this time -- especially for you. 
Can you ride? 
It will be quicker this way.
###DIALOGUE###``My name is FIRENZE,'' HARRY added, as HARRY lowered himself on to HARRY's front legs so that HARRY could clamber onto HARRY's back.
There was suddenly a sound of more galloping from the other side of the clearing. 
RONAN and BANE came bursting through the trees, their flanks heaving and sweaty.
###DIALOGUE###``FIRENZE!'' 
BANE thundered. 
###DIALOGUE###``What are you doing? 
###DIALOGUE###You have a human on your back! 
###DIALOGUE###Have you no shame? 
###DIALOGUE###Are you a common mule?''
###DIALOGUE###``Do you realize who this is?'' said FIRENZE. 
###DIALOGUE###``This is the HARRY boy. 
###DIALOGUE###The quicker HARRY leaves this forest, the better.''
###DIALOGUE###``What have you been telling HARRY?'' growled BANE. 
###DIALOGUE###``Remember, FIRENZE, we are sworn not to set ourselves against the heavens. 
###DIALOGUE###Have we not read what is to come in the movements of the planets?''
RONAN pawed the ground nervously. 
###DIALOGUE###``I'm sure FIRENZE thought HARRY was acting for the best, '' RONAN said in RONAN's gloomy voice.
BANE kicked RONAN's back legs in anger.
###DIALOGUE###``For the best! 
###DIALOGUE###What is that to do with us? 
###DIALOGUE###Centaurs are concerned with what has been foretold! 
###DIALOGUE###It is not our business to run around like donkeys after stray humans in our forest!''
FIRENZE suddenly reared on to RONAN's hind legs in anger, so that HARRY had to grab HARRY's shoulders to stay on.
###DIALOGUE###``Do you not see that unicorn?'' 
FIRENZE bellowed at BANE. 
###DIALOGUE###``Do you not understand why it was killed? 
###DIALOGUE###Or have the planets not let you in on that secret? 
###DIALOGUE###I set myself against what is lurking in this forest, BANE, yes, with humans alongside me if I must.''
And FIRENZE whisked around; with HARRY clutching on as best HARRY could, they plunged off into the trees, leaving RONAN and BANE behind them.
HARRY didn't have a clue what was going on.
###DIALOGUE###``Why's BANE so angry?'' 
HARRY asked. 
###DIALOGUE###``What was that thing you saved me from, anyway?''
FIRENZE slowed to a walk, warned HARRY to keep HARRY's head bowed in case of low-hanging branches, but did not answer HARRY's question. 
They made their way through the trees in silence for so long that HARRY thought FIRENZE didn't want to talk to HARRY anymore. 
They were passing through a particularly dense patch of trees, however, when FIRENZE suddenly stopped.
###DIALOGUE###``HARRY , do you know what unicorn blood is used -for?''
###DIALOGUE###``No,'' said HARRY, startled by the odd question. 
###DIALOGUE###``We've only used the horn and tail hair in Potions.''
###DIALOGUE###``That is because it is a monstrous thing, to slay a unicorn,'' said FIRENZE. 
###DIALOGUE###``Only one who has nothing to lose, and everything to gain, would commit such a crime. 
###DIALOGUE###The blood of a unicorn will keep you alive, even if you are an inch from death, but at a terrible price. 
###DIALOGUE###You have slain something pure and defenseless to save yourself, and you will have but a half-life, a cursed life, from the moment the blood touches your lips.''
HARRY stared at the back of FIRENZE's head, which was dappled silver in the moonlight.
###DIALOGUE###``But who'd be that desperate?'' 
HARRY wondered aloud. 
###DIALOGUE###``If you're going to be cursed forever, deaths better, isn't it?''
###DIALOGUE###``It is,'' FIRENZE agreed, ``unless all you need is to stay alive long enough to drink something else -- something that will bring you back to full strength and power -- something that will mean you can never die.
###DIALOGUE###HARRY , do you know what is hidden in the school at this very moment?''
###DIALOGUE###``The Sorcerer's Stone! 
###DIALOGUE###Of course -- the Elixir of Life! 
###DIALOGUE###But I don't understand who --''
###DIALOGUE###``Can you think of nobody who has waited many years to return to power, who has clung to life, awaiting their chance?''
It was as though an iRON fist had clenched suddenly around HARRY's heart. 
###DIALOGUE###Over the rustling of the trees, HARRY seemed to hear once more what HAGRID had told HARRY on the night they had met: ``Some say he died.
Codswallop, in my opinion. 
###DIALOGUE###Dunno if he had enough human left in him to die.''
###DIALOGUE###``Do you mean,'' HARRY croaked, ``that was Vol-''
###DIALOGUE###``HARRY! 
###DIALOGUE###HARRY, are you all right?''
HERMIONE was running toward them down the path, HAGRID puffing along behind HERMIONE.
###DIALOGUE###``I'm fine,'' said HARRY, hardly knowing what HARRY was saying. 
###DIALOGUE###``The unicorn's dead, HAGRID, it's in that clearing back there.''
###DIALOGUE###``This is where I leave you,'' FIRENZE murmured as HAGRID hurried off to examine the unicorn. 
###DIALOGUE###``You are safe now.''
HARRY slid off HARRY's back.
###DIALOGUE###``Good luck, HARRY ,'' said FIRENZE. 
###DIALOGUE###``The planets have been read wrongly before now, even by centaurs. 
###DIALOGUE###I hope this is one of those times.''
HARRY turned and cantered back into the depths of the forest, leaving HARRY shivering behind HARRY.
RON had fallen asleep in the dark common room, waiting for them to return. 
RON shouted something about Quidditch fouls when HARRY roughly shook HARRY awake. 
In a matter of seconds, though, HARRY was wide-eyed as HARRY began to tell HARRY and HERMIONE what had happened in the forest.
HARRY couldn't sit down. 
He paced up and down in front of the fire. 
He was still shaking.
###DIALOGUE###``SNAPE wants the stone for VOLDEMORT... and VOLDEMORT's waiting in the forest... and all this time we thought SNAPE just wanted to get rich...''
###DIALOGUE###``Stop saying the name!'' said RON in a terrified whisper, as if RON thought VOLDEMORT could hear them.
HARRY wasn't listening.
###DIALOGUE###``FIRENZE saved me, but SNAPE shouldn't have done so... BANE was furious...
###DIALOGUE###SNAPE was talking about interfering with what the planets say is going to happen... They must show that VOLDEMORT's coming back... BANE thinks FIRENZE should have let VOLDEMORT kill me... I suppose that's written in the stars as well.''
###DIALOGUE###``Will you stop saying the name!'' 
RON hissed.
###DIALOGUE###``So all I've got to wait for now is SNAPE to steal the Stone,'' HARRY went on feverishly, ``then VOLDEMORT will be able to come and finish me off... Well, I suppose BANE'll be happy.''
HERMIONE looked very frightened, but HERMIONE had a word of comfort.
###DIALOGUE###``HARRY, everyone says DUMBLEDORE's the only one YOU-KNOW-WHO was ever afraid of With DUMBLEDORE around, YOU-KNOW-WHO won't touch you. 
###DIALOGUE###Anyway, who says the centaurs are right? 
###DIALOGUE###It sounds like fortune-telling to me, and MCGONAGALL says that's a very imprecise branch of magic.''
The sky had turned light before they stopped talking. 
They went to bed exhausted, their throats sore. 
But the night's surprises weren't over.
When HARRY pulled back HARRY's sheets, HARRY found HARRY's invisibility cloak folded neatly underneath them. 
There was a note pinned to it: Just in case.
CHAPTER SIXTEEN
THROUGH THE TRAPDOOR
In years to come, HARRY would never quite remember how HARRY had managed to get through HARRY's exams when HARRY half expected VOLDEMORT to come bursting through the door at any moment. 
Yet the days crept by, and there could be no doubt that FLUFFY was still alive and well behind the locked door.
It was sweltering hot, especially in the large classroom where they did their written papers. 
They had been given special, new quills for the exams, which had been bewitched with an AntiCheating spell.
They had practical exams as well. 
FLITWICK called them one by one into his class to see if they could make a pineapple tapdance across a desk. 
MCGONAGALL watched them turn a mouse into a snuffbox -- points were given for how pretty the snuffbox was, but taken away if it had whiskers. 
SNAPE made them all nervous, breathing down their necks while they tried to remember how to make a Forgetfulness potion.
HARRY did the best HARRY could, trying to ignore the stabbing pains in HARRY's forehead, which had been bothering HARRY ever since HARRY's trip into the forest. 
NEVILLE thought HARRY had a bad case of exam nerves because HARRY couldn't sleep, but the truth was that HARRY kept being woken by HARRY's old nightmare, except that it was now worse than ever because there was a hooded figure dripping blood in it.
Maybe it was because they hadn't seen what HARRY had seen in the forest, or because they didn't have scars burning on their foreheads, but RON and HERMIONE didn't seem as worried about the Stone as HARRY. 
The idea of VOLDEMORT certainly scared them, but HARRY didn't keep visiting them in dreams, and they were so busy with their studying they didn't have much time to fret about what SNAPE or anyone else might be up to.
Their very last exam was History of Magic. 
One hour of answering questions about batty old wizards who'd invented selfstirring cauldRONs and they'd be free, free for a whole wonderful week until their exam results came out. 
When the ghost of BINNS told them to put down their quills and roll up their parchment, HARRY couldn't help cheering with the rest.
###DIALOGUE###``That was far easier than I thought it would be,'' said HERMIONE as they joined the crowds flocking out onto the sunny grounds. 
###DIALOGUE###``I needn't have learned about the 1637 Werewolf Code of Conduct or the uprising of Elfric the Eager.''
HERMIONE always liked to go through their exam papers afterward, but RON said this made RON feel ill, so they wandered down to the lake and flopped under a tree. 
The PERCY twins and LEE were tickling the tentacles of a giant squid, which was basking in the warm shallows. 
###DIALOGUE###``No more studying,'' RON sighed happily, stretching out on the grass. 
###DIALOGUE###``You could look more cheerful, HARRY, we've got a week before we find out how badly we've done, there's no need to worry yet.''
HARRY was rubbing HARRY's forehead.
###DIALOGUE###``I wish I knew what this means!'' 
HARRY burst out angrily. 
###DIALOGUE###``My scar keeps hurting -- it's happened before, but never as often as this.''
###DIALOGUE###``Go to Madam Pomfrey,'' HERMIONE suggested.
###DIALOGUE###``I'm not ill,'' said HARRY. 
###DIALOGUE###``I think it's a warning... it means danger's coming...''
RON couldn't get worked up, it was too hot.
###DIALOGUE###``HARRY, relax, HERMIONE's right, the Stone's safe as long as DUMBLEDORE's around. 
###DIALOGUE###Anyway, we've never had any proof SNAPE found out how to get past Fluffy. 
###DIALOGUE###SNAPE nearly had SNAPE's leg ripped off once, SNAPE's not going to try it again in a hurry. 
###DIALOGUE###And NEVILLE will play Quidditch for England before HAGRID lets DUMBLEDORE down.''
HARRY nodded, but HARRY couldn't shake off a lurking feeling that there was something HARRY'd forgotten to do, something important. 
###DIALOGUE###When HARRY tried to explain this, HERMIONE said, ``That's just the exams.

###DIALOGUE###``Do you think they'll attack us if we cross the room?'' said RON.
###DIALOGUE###``Probably,'' said HARRY. 
###DIALOGUE###``They don't look very vicious, but I suppose if they all swooped down at once... well, there's no other choice... I'll run.''
HARRY took a deep breath, covered HARRY's face with HARRY's arms, and sprinted across the room. 
HARRY expected to feel sharp beaks and claws tearing at HARRY any second, but nothing happened. 
HARRY reached the door untouched. 
HARRY pulled the handle, but it was locked.
The other two followed HARRY. 
They tugged and heaved at the door, but it wouldn't budge, not even when HERMIONE tried HERMIONE's Alohomora charm.
###DIALOGUE###``Now what?'' said RON.
###DIALOGUE###``These birds... they can't be here just for decoration,'' said HERMIONE.
They watched the birds soaring overhead, glittering -- glittering? 
###DIALOGUE###``They're not birds!'' 
HARRY said suddenly. 
###DIALOGUE###``They're keys! 
###DIALOGUE###Winged keys -- look carefully. 
###DIALOGUE###So that must mean...'' HARRY looked around the chamber while the other two squinted up at the flock of keys. ''
###DIALOGUE###... yes -- look! 
###DIALOGUE###Broomsticks! 
###DIALOGUE###We've got to catch the key to the door!''
###DIALOGUE###``But there are hundreds of them!''
RON examined the lock on the door.
###DIALOGUE###``We're looking for a big, old-fashioned one -- probably silver, like the handle.''
They each seized a broomstick and kicked off into the air, soaring into the midst of the cloud of keys. 
They grabbed and snatched, but the bewitched keys darted and dived so quickly it was almost impossible to catch one.
Not for nothing, though, was HARRY the youngest Seeker in a century. 
HARRY had a knack for spotting things other people didn't. 
After a minute's weaving about through the whirl of rainbow feathers, HARRY noticed a large silver key that had a bent wing, as if it had already been caught and stuffed roughly into the keyhole.
###DIALOGUE###``That one!'' 
HARRY called to the others. 
###DIALOGUE###``That big one -- there -- no, there -- with bright blue wings -- the feathers are all crumpled on one side.''
RON went speeding in the direction that HARRY was pointing, crashed into the ceiling, and nearly fell off HARRY's broom.
###DIALOGUE###``We've got to close in on it!'' 
HARRY called, not taking HARRY's eyes off the key with the damaged wing. 
###DIALOGUE###``RON, you come at it from above -- HERMIONE, stay below and stop it from going down and I'll try and catch it. 
###DIALOGUE###Right, NOW!''
RON dived, HERMIONE rocketed upward, the key dodged them both, and HARRY streaked after it; it sped toward the wall, HARRY leaned forward and with a nasty, crunching noise, pinned it against the stone with one hand. 
RON and HERMIONE's cheers echoed around the high chamber.
They landed quickly, and HARRY ran to the door, the key struggling in HARRY's hand. 
HARRY rammed it into the lock and turned -- it worked. 
The moment the lock had clicked open, the key took flight again, looking very battered now that it had been caught twice.
###DIALOGUE###``Ready?'' 
HARRY asked the other two, HARRY's hand on the door handle. 
They nodded. 
HARRY pulled the door open.
The next chamber was so dark they couldn't see anything at all. 
But as they stepped into it, light suddenly flooded the room to reveal an astonishing sight.
They were standing on the edge of a huge chessboard, behind the black chessmen, which were all taller than they were and carved from what looked like black stone. 
Facing them, way across the chamber, were the white pieces. 
HARRY, RON and HERMIONE shivered slightly -- the towering white chessmen had no faces.
###DIALOGUE###``Now what do we do?'' 
HARRY whispered.
###DIALOGUE###``It's obvious, isn't it?'' said RON. 
###DIALOGUE###``We've got to play our way across the room.''
Behind the white pieces they could see another door.
###DIALOGUE###``How?'' said HERMIONE nervously.
###DIALOGUE###``I think,'' said RON, ``we're going to have to be chessmen.''
RON walked up to a black knight and put RON's hand out to touch the knight's horse. 
At once, the stone sprang to life. 
The horse pawed the ground and the knight turned his helmeted head to look down at RON.
###DIALOGUE###``Do we -- er -- have to join you to get across?'' 
The black knight nodded. 
RON turned to the other two.
###DIALOGUE###``This needs thinking about he said. 
###DIALOGUE###I suppose we've got to take the place of three of the black pieces...''
HARRY and HERMIONE stayed quiet, watching RON think. 
###DIALOGUE###Finally RON said, ``Now, don't be offended or anything, but neither of you are that good at chess --''
###DIALOGUE###``We're not offended,'' said HARRY quickly. 
###DIALOGUE###``Just tell us what to do.''
###DIALOGUE###``Well, HARRY, you take the place of that bishop, and HERMIONE, YOU 90 next to HARRY instead of that castle.''
###DIALOGUE###``What about you?''
###DIALOGUE###``I'm going to be a knight,'' said RON.
The chessmen seemed to have been listening, because at these words a knight, a bishop, and a castle turned their backs on the white pieces and walked off the board, leaving three empty squares that HARRY, RON, and HERMIONE took.
###DIALOGUE###``White always plays first in chess,'' said RON, peering across the board.
###DIALOGUE###``Yes... look...''
A white pawn had moved forward two squares.
RON started to direct the black pieces. 
They moved silently wherever RON sent them. 
HARRY's knees were trembling. 
What if they lost? 
###DIALOGUE###``HARRY -- move diagonally four squares to the right.''
Their first real shock came when their other knight was taken. 
The white queen smashed him to the floor and dragged him off the board, where he lay quite still, facedown.
###DIALOGUE###``Had to let that happen,'' said RON, looking shaken. 
###DIALOGUE###``Leaves you free to take that bishop, HERMIONE, go on.''
Every time one of their men was lost, the white pieces showed no mercy.
Soon there was a huddle of limp black players slumped along the wall.
Twice, RON only just noticed in time that HARRY and HERMIONE were in danger. 
HARRY himself darted around the board, taking almost as many white pieces as they had lost black ones.
###DIALOGUE###``We're nearly there,'' HARRY muttered suddenly. 
###DIALOGUE###``Let me think let me think...''
The white queen turned her blank face toward HARRY.
###DIALOGUE###``Yes...'' said RON softly, ``It's the only way... I've got to be taken.''
###DIALOGUE###``NOF HARRY and HERMIONE shouted.
###DIALOGUE###``That's chess!'' snapped RON. 
###DIALOGUE###``You've got to make some sacrifices! 
###DIALOGUE###I take one step forward and HERMIONE'll take me -- that leaves you free to checkmate the king, HARRY!''
###DIALOGUE###``But --''
###DIALOGUE###``Do you want to stop SNAPE or not?''
###DIALOGUE###``RON --''
###DIALOGUE###``Look, if you don't hurry up, RON'll already have the Stone!''
There was no alternative.
###DIALOGUE###``Ready?'' 
RON called, RON's face pale but determined. 
###DIALOGUE###``Here I go - now, don't hang around once you've won.''
RON stepped forward, and the white queen pounced. 
She struck RON hard across the head with her stone arm, and RON crashed to the floor - HERMIONE screamed but stayed on HERMIONE's square - the white queen dragged RON to one side. 
RON looked as if RON'd been knocked out.
Shaking, HARRY moved three spaces to the left.
The white king took off HARRY's crown and threw it at HARRY's feet. 
They had won. 
The chessmen parted and bowed, leaving the door ahead clear. 
With one last desperate look back at RON, HARRY and HERMIONE charged through the door and up the next passageway.
###DIALOGUE###``What if RON's --?''
###DIALOGUE###``RON'll be all right,'' said HARRY, trying to convince himself. 
###DIALOGUE###``What do you reckon's next?''
###DIALOGUE###``We've had Sprout's, that was the Devil's Snare; FLITWICK must've put charms on the keys; MCGONAGALL transfigured the chessmen to make them alive; that leaves QUIRRELL's spell, and SNAPE's.''
They had reached another door.
###DIALOGUE###``All right?'' 
HARRY whispered.
###DIALOGUE###``Go on.''
HARRY pushed it open.
A disgusting smell filled their nostrils, making both of them pull their robes up over their noses. 
Eyes watering, they saw, flat on the floor in front of them, a troll even larger than the one they had tackled, out cold with a bloody lump on its head.
###DIALOGUE###``I'm glad we didn't have to fight that one,'' HARRY whispered as they stepped carefully over one of its massive legs. 
###DIALOGUE###``Come on, I can't breathe.''
HARRY pulled open the next door, both of them hardly daring to look at what came next - but there was nothing very frightening in here, just a table with seven differently shaped bottles standing on it in a line.
###DIALOGUE###``SNAPE's,'' said HARRY. 
###DIALOGUE###``What do we have to do?''
They stepped over the threshold, and immediately a fire sprang up behind them in the doorway. 
It wasn't ordinary fire either; it was purple. 
At the same instant, black flames shot up in the doorway leading onward.
They were trapped.
###DIALOGUE###``Look!'' 
HERMIONE seized a roll of paper lying next to the bottles. 
HARRY looked over HERMIONE's shoulder to read it: Danger lies before you, while safety lies behind, Two of us will help you, which ever you would find, One among us seven will let you move ahead, Another will transport the drinker back instead, Two among our number hold only nettle wine, Three of us are killers, waiting bidden in line.
Choose, unless you wish to stay here forevermore, To help you in your choice, we give you these clues four: First, however slyly the poison tries to hide You will always find some on nettle wine's left side; Second, different are those who stand at either end, But if you would move onward, neither is your friend; Third, as you see clearly, all are different size, Neither dwarf nor giant holds death in their insides; Fourth, the second left and the second on the right Are twins once you taste them, though different at first sight.
HERMIONE let out a great sigh and HARRY, amazed, saw that HERMIONE was smiling, the very last thing HARRY felt like doing.
###DIALOGUE###``Brilliant,'' said HERMIONE. 
###DIALOGUE###``This isn't magic -- it's logic -- a puzzle.
###DIALOGUE###A lot of the greatest wizards haven't got an ounce of logic, they'd be stuck in here forever.''
###DIALOGUE###``But so will we, won't we?'' 
###DIALOGUE###``Of course not,'' said HERMIONE. 
###DIALOGUE###``Everything we need is here on this paper. 
###DIALOGUE###Seven bottles: three are poison; two are wine; one will get us safely through the black fire, and one will get us back through the purple.''
###DIALOGUE###``But how do we know which to drink?''
###DIALOGUE###``Give me a minute.''
HERMIONE read the paper several times. 
Then HERMIONE walked up and down the line of bottles, muttering to herself and pointing at them. 
At last, HERMIONE clapped HERMIONE's hands.
###DIALOGUE###``Got it,'' HERMIONE said. 
###DIALOGUE###``The smallest bottle will get us through the black fire -- toward the Stone.''
HARRY looked at the tiny bottle.
###DIALOGUE###``There's only enough there for one of us,'' HARRY said. 
###DIALOGUE###``That's hardly one swallow.''
They looked at each other.
###DIALOGUE###``Which one will get you back through the purple flames?''
HERMIONE pointed at a rounded bottle at the right end of the line.
###DIALOGUE###``You drink that,'' said HARRY. 
###DIALOGUE###``No, listen, get back and get RON. 
###DIALOGUE###Grab brooms from the flying- key room, they'll get you out of the trapdoor and past Fluffy -- go straight to the owlery and send HEDWIG to DUMBLEDORE, we need DUMBLEDORE. 
###DIALOGUE###I might be able to hold SNAPE off for a while, but I'm no match for SNAPE, really.''
###DIALOGUE###``But HARRY -- what if YOU-KNOW-WHO's with HARRY?''
###DIALOGUE###``Well -- I was lucky once, wasn't I?'' said HARRY, pointing at HARRY's scar.
###DIALOGUE###``I might get lucky again.''
HERMIONE's lip trembled, and HERMIONE suddenly dashed at HARRY and threw HERMIONE's arms around HARRY.
###DIALOGUE###``HERMIONE!''
###DIALOGUE###``HARRY -- you're a great wizard, you know.''
###DIALOGUE###``I'm not as good as you,'' said HARRY, very embarrassed, as HERMIONE let go of HARRY.
###DIALOGUE###``Me!'' said HERMIONE. 
###DIALOGUE###``Books! 
###DIALOGUE###And cleverness! 
###DIALOGUE###There are more important things -- friendship and bravery and -- oh HARRY -- be careful!''
###DIALOGUE###``You drink first,'' said HARRY. 
###DIALOGUE###``You are sure which is which, aren't you?''
###DIALOGUE###``Positive,'' said HERMIONE. 
HERMIONE took a long drink from the round bottle at the end, and shuddered.
###DIALOGUE###``It's not poison?'' said HARRY anxiously.
###DIALOGUE###``No -- but it's like ice.''
###DIALOGUE###``Quick, go, before it wears off.''
###DIALOGUE###``Good luck -- take care.''
###DIALOGUE###``GO!''
HERMIONE turned and walked straight through the purple fire.
HARRY took a deep breath and picked up the smallest bottle. 
HARRY turned to face the black flames.
###DIALOGUE###``Here I come,'' HARRY said, and HARRY drained the little bottle in one gulp.
It was indeed as though ice was flooding HARRY's body. 
HARRY put the bottle down and walked forward; HARRY braced himself, saw the black flames licking HARRY's body, but couldn't feel them -- for a moment HARRY could see nothing but dark fire -- then HARRY was on the other side, in the last chamber.
There was already someone there -- but it wasn't SNAPE. 
It wasn't even VOLDEMORT.
CHAPTER SEVENTEEN
THE MAN WITH TWO FACES It was QUIRRELL.
###DIALOGUE###``You!'' gasped HARRY.
QUIRRELL smiled. 
HARRY's face wasn't twitching at all.
###DIALOGUE###``Me,'' HARRY said calmly. 
###DIALOGUE###``I wondered whether I'd be meeting you here, HARRY.''
###DIALOGUE###``But I thought -- SNAPE --''
###DIALOGUE###``SNAPE?'' 
QUIRRELL laughed, and it wasn't HARRY's usual quivering treble, either, but cold and sharp. 
###DIALOGUE###``Yes, SNAPE does seem the type, doesn't SNAPE? 
###DIALOGUE###So useful to have SNAPE swooping around like an overgrown bat. 
###DIALOGUE###Next to SNAPE, who would suspect p-p-poor, st-stuttering P-QUIRRELL?''
HARRY couldn't take it in. 
This couldn't be true, it couldn't.
###DIALOGUE###``But SNAPE tried to kill me!''
###DIALOGUE###``No, no, no. 
###DIALOGUE###I tried to kill you. 
###DIALOGUE###Your friend HERMIONE accidentally knocked me over as HERMIONE rushed to set fire to SNAPE at that Quidditch match. 
###DIALOGUE###HERMIONE broke my eye contact with you. 
###DIALOGUE###Another few seconds and I'd have got you off that broom. 
###DIALOGUE###I'd have managed it before then if SNAPE hadn't been muttering a countercurse, trying to save you.''
###DIALOGUE###``SNAPE was trying to save me?''
###DIALOGUE###``Of course,'' said QUIRRELL coolly. ''
###DIALOGUE###\Why do you think HARRY wanted to referee your next match? 
###DIALOGUE###HARRY was trying to make sure I didn't do it again. 
###DIALOGUE###Funny, really... HARRY needn't have bothered. 
###DIALOGUE###I couldn't do anything with DUMBLEDORE watching. 
###DIALOGUE###All the other teachers thought SNAPE was trying to stop GRYFFINDOR from winning, SNAPE did make himself unpopular...
###DIALOGUE###and what a waste of time, when after all that, I'm going to kill you tonight.''
QUIRRELL snapped SNAPE's fingers. 
Ropes sprang out of thin air and wrapped themselves tightly around HARRY.
###DIALOGUE###``You're too nosy to live, HARRY. 
###DIALOGUE###Scurrying around the school on Halloween like that, for all I knew you'd seen me coming to look at what was guarding the Stone.''
###DIALOGUE###``You let the troll in?''
###DIALOGUE###``Certainly. 
###DIALOGUE###I have a special gift with trolls -- you must have seen what I did to the one in the chamber back there? 
###DIALOGUE###Unfortunately, while everyone else was running around looking for it, SNAPE, who already suspected me, went straight to the third floor to head me off -- and not only did my troll fail to beat you to death, that three-headed dog didn't even manage to bite SNAPE's leg off properly.
###DIALOGUE###``Now, wait quietly, HARRY. 
###DIALOGUE###I need to examine this interesting mirror.
It was only then that HARRY realized what was standing behind QUIRRELL.
It was the Mirror of Erised.
###DIALOGUE###``This mirror is the key to finding the Stone,'' QUIRRELL murmured, tapping HARRY's way around the frame. 
###DIALOGUE###``Trust DUMBLEDORE to come up with something like this... but DUMBLEDORE's in London... I'll be far away by the time DUMBLEDORE gets back...''
All HARRY could think of doing was to keep QUIRRELL talking and stop him from concentrating on the mirror.
###DIALOGUE###``I saw you and SNAPE in the forest --'' he blurted out.
###DIALOGUE###``Yes,'' said QUIRRELL idly, walking around the mirror to look at the back. 
###DIALOGUE###``SNAPE was on to me by that time, trying to find out how far I'd got.
SNAPE suspected me all along. 
###DIALOGUE###Tried to frighten me - as though SNAPE could, when I had VOLDEMORT on my side...''
QUIRRELL came back out from behind the mirror and stared hungrily into it.
###DIALOGUE###``I see the Stone... I'm presenting it to my master... but where is it?''
HARRY struggled against the ropes binding HARRY, but they didn't give. 
HARRY had to keep QUIRRELL from giving HARRY's whole attention to the mirror.
###DIALOGUE###``But SNAPE always seemed to hate me so much.''
###DIALOGUE###``Oh, SNAPE does,'' said QUIRRELL casually, ``heavens, yes. 
###DIALOGUE###SNAPE was at HOGWARTS with your father, didn't you know? 
###DIALOGUE###They loathed each other. 
###DIALOGUE###But SNAPE never wanted you dead.''
###DIALOGUE###``But I heard you a few days ago, sobbing -- I thought SNAPE was threatening you...''
For the first time, a spasm of fear flitted across QUIRRELL's face.
###DIALOGUE###``Sometimes,'' HARRY said, ``I find it hard to follow my master's instructions -- SNAPE is a great wizard and I am weak --''
###DIALOGUE###``You mean SNAPE was there in the classroom with you?'' 
HARRY gasped.
###DIALOGUE###``SNAPE is with me wherever I go,'' said QUIRRELL quietly. 
###DIALOGUE###``I met SNAPE when I traveled around the world. 
###DIALOGUE###A foolish young man I was then, full of ridiculous ideas about good and evil. 
###DIALOGUE###VOLDEMORT showed me how wrong I was. 
###DIALOGUE###There is no good and evil, there is only power, and those too weak to seek it... Since then, I have served VOLDEMORT faithfully, although I have let VOLDEMORT down many times. 
###DIALOGUE###VOLDEMORT has had to be very hard on me.''
QUIRRELL shivered suddenly. 
###DIALOGUE###``VOLDEMORT does not forgive mistakes easily. 
###DIALOGUE###When I failed to steal the stone from GRINGOTTS, VOLDEMORT was most displeased. 
###DIALOGUE###VOLDEMORT punished me... decided VOLDEMORT would have to keep a closer watch on me...''
QUIRRELL's voice trailed away. 
HARRY was remembering HARRY's trip to Diagon Alley -how could HARRY have been so stupid? 
HARRY'd seen QUIRRELL there that very day, shaken hands with HARRY in the Leaky Cauldron.
QUIRRELL cursed under HARRY's breath.
###DIALOGUE###``I don't understand... is the Stone inside the mirror? 
###DIALOGUE###Should I break it?''
HARRY's mind was racing.
What I want more than anything else in the world at the moment, HARRY thought, is to find the Stone before QUIRRELL does. 
So if I look in the mirror, I should see myseff finding it -- which means I'll see where it's hidden! 
But how can I look without QUIRRELL realizing what I'm up to? 
HARRY tried to edge to the left, to get in front of the glass without QUIRRELL noticing, but the ropes around HARRY's ankles were too tight: HARRY tripped and fell over. 
QUIRRELL ignored HARRY. 
HARRY was still talking to himself. 
###DIALOGUE###``What does this mirror do? 
###DIALOGUE###How does it work? 
###DIALOGUE###Help me, Master!''
###DIALOGUE###And to HARRY's horror, a voice answered, and the voice seemed to come from QUIRRELL himself ``Use the boy... Use the boy...''
QUIRRELL rounded on HARRY.
###DIALOGUE###``Yes -- HARRY -- come here.''
HARRY clapped HARRY's hands once, and the ropes binding HARRY fell off. 
HARRY got slowly to HARRY's feet.
###DIALOGUE###``Come here,'' QUIRRELL repeated. 
###DIALOGUE###``Look in the mirror and tell me what you see.''
HARRY walked toward HARRY.
I must lie, HARRY thought desperately. 
I must look and lie about what I see, that's all.
QUIRRELL moved close behind HARRY. 
HARRY breathed in the funny smell that seemed to come from QUIRRELL's turban. 
HARRY closed HARRY's eyes, stepped in front of the mirror, and opened them again.
HARRY saw HARRY's reflection, pale and scared-looking at first. 
But a moment later, the reflection smiled at HARRY. 
It put its hand into its pocket and pulled out a blood-red stone. 
It winked and put the Stone back in its pocket -- and as it did so, HARRY felt something heavy drop into HARRY's real pocket. 
Somehow -- incredibly -- HARRY'd gotten the Stone.
###DIALOGUE###``Well?'' said QUIRRELL impatiently. 
###DIALOGUE###``What do you see?''
HARRY screwed up HARRY's courage.
###DIALOGUE###``I see myself shaking hands with DUMBLEDORE,'' HARRY invented. 
###DIALOGUE###``I -- I've won the house cup for GRYFFINDOR.''
QUIRRELL cursed again.
###DIALOGUE###``Get out of the way,'' HARRY said. 
As HARRY moved aside, HARRY felt the Sorcerer's Stone against HARRY's leg. 
Dare HARRY make a break for it? 
But HARRY hadn't walked five paces before a high voice spoke, though QUIRRELL wasn't moving HARRY's lips.
###DIALOGUE###``DUMBLEDORE lies... DUMBLEDORE lies...''
###DIALOGUE###``HARRY, come back here!'' 
QUIRRELL shouted. 
###DIALOGUE###``Tell me the truth! 
###DIALOGUE###What did you just see?''
The high voice spoke again.
###DIALOGUE###``Let me speak to HARRY... face-to-face...''
###DIALOGUE###``Master, you are not strong enough!''
###DIALOGUE###``I have strength enough... for this...''
HARRY felt as if Devil's Snare was rooting HARRY to the spot. 
HARRY couldn't move a muscle. 
Petrified, HARRY watched as QUIRRELL reached up and began to unwrap HARRY's turban. 
What was going on? 
The turban fell away. 
QUIRRELL's head looked strangely small without it. 
Then HARRY turned slowly on the spot.
HARRY would have screamed, but HARRY couldn't make a sound. 
Where there should have been a back to QUIRRELL's head, there was a face, the most terrible face HARRY had ever seen. 
It was chalk white with glaring red eyes and slits for nostrils, like a snake.
###DIALOGUE###``HARRY ...'' it whispered.
HARRY tried to take a step backward but HARRY's legs wouldn't move.
###DIALOGUE###``See what I have become?'' the face said. 
###DIALOGUE###``Mere shadow and vapor ... I have form only when I can share another's body... but there have always been those willing to let me into their hearts and minds... Unicorn blood has strengthened me, these past weeks... you saw faithful QUIRRELL drinking it for me in the forest... and once I have the Elixir of Life, I will be able to create a body of my own... Now... why don't you give me that Stone in your pocket?''
So HARRY knew. 
The feeling suddenly surged back into HARRY's legs. 
HARRY stumbled backward.
###DIALOGUE###``Don't be a fool,'' snarled the face. 
###DIALOGUE###``Better save your own life and join me... or you'll meet the same end as your parents... They died begging me for mercy...''
###DIALOGUE###``LIAR!'' 
HARRY shouted suddenly.
QUIRRELL was walking backward at HARRY, so that VOLDEMORT could still see VOLDEMORT. 
The evil face was now smiling.
###DIALOGUE###``How touching...'' it hissed. 
###DIALOGUE###``I always value bravery... Yes, boy, your parents were brave... I killed your father first; and he put up a courageous fight... but your mother needn't have died... she was trying to protect you... Now give me the Stone, unless you want her to have died in vain.''
###DIALOGUE###``NEVER!''
###DIALOGUE###HARRY sprang toward the flame door, but VOLDEMORT screamed ``SEIZE HIM!'' and the next second, HARRY felt QUIRRELL's hand close on HARRY's wrist. 
At once, a needle-sharp pain seared across HARRY's scar; HARRY's head felt as though it was about to split in two; HARRY yelled, struggling with all HARRY's might, and to HARRY's surprise, QUIRRELL let go of HARRY. 
The pain in HARRY's head lessened -- HARRY looked around wildly to see where QUIRRELL had gone, and saw HARRY hunched in pain, looking at HARRY's fingers -- they were blistering before HARRY's eyes.
###DIALOGUE###``Seize him! 
###DIALOGUE###SEIZE HIM!'' shrieked VOLDEMORT again, and QUIRRELL lunged, knocking HARRY clean off HARRY's feet' landing on top of HARRY, both hands around HARRY's neck -- HARRY's scar was almost blinding HARRY with pain, yet HARRY could see QUIRRELL howling in agony.
###DIALOGUE###``Master, I cannot hold him -- my hands -- my hands!''
And QUIRRELL, though pinning HARRY to the ground with HARRY's knees, let go of HARRY's neck and stared, bewildered, at HARRY's own palms -- HARRY could see they looked burned, raw, red, and shiny.
###DIALOGUE###``Then kill him, fool, and be done!'' screeched VOLDEMORT.
###DIALOGUE###QUIRRELL raised HARRY's hand to perform a deadly curse, but HARRY, by instinct, reached up and grabbed QUIRRELL's face -- ``AAAARGH!''
QUIRRELL rolled off HARRY, HARRY's face blistering, too, and then HARRY knew: QUIRRELL couldn't touch HARRY's bare skin, not without suffering terrible pain -- HARRY's only chance was to keep hold of QUIRRELL, keep HARRY in enough pain to stop HARRY from doing a curse.
HARRY jumped to HARRY's feet, caught QUIRRELL by the arm, and hung on as tight as HARRY could. 
###DIALOGUE###QUIRRELL screamed and tried to throw HARRY off -- the pain in HARRY's head was building -- HARRY couldn't see -- HARRY could only hear QUIRRELL's terrible shrieks and VOLDEMORT's yells of, ``KILL HIM! 
###DIALOGUE###KILL HIM!'' and other voices, maybe in HARRY's own head, crying, ``HARRY!

HARRY had been held up by POMFREY 's fussing about, insisting on giving HARRY one last checkup, so the Great Hall was already full. 
It was decked out in the SLYTHERIN colors of green and silver to celebrate SLYTHERIN's winning the house cup for the seventh year in a row. 
A huge banner showing the SLYTHERIN serpent covered the wall behind the High Table.
When HARRY walked in there was a sudden hush, and then everybody started talking loudly at once.

The babble died away.
###DIALOGUE###``Another year gone!'' DUMBLEDORE said cheerfully.

###DIALOGUE###The room went deadly quiet for pure nerve and outstanding courage, I award GRYFFINDOR house sixty points.''

Those who could add up while yelling themselves hoarse knew that GRYFFINDOR now had four hundred and seventy-two points -- exactly the same as SLYTHERIN.

Someone standing outside the Great Hall might well have thought some sort of explosion had taken place, so loud was the noise that erupted from the GRYFFINDOR table.

NEVILLE had never won so much as a point for GRYFFINDOR before.

###DIALOGUE###``Which means, DUMBLEDORE called over the storm of applause, for even RAVENCLAW and HUFFLEPUFF were celebrating the downfall of SLYTHERIN, ``we need a little change of decoration.''
He clapped his hands. 
In an instant, the green hangings became scarlet and the silver became gold; the huge SLYTHERIN serpent vanished and a towering GRYFFINDOR lion took its place. 
SNAPE was shaking MCGONAGALL's hand, with a horrible, forced smile. 
SNAPE caught HARRY's eye and HARRY knew at once that SNAPE's feelings toward HARRY hadn't changed one jot. 
This didn't worry HARRY. 
It seemed as though life would be back to normal next year, or as normal as it ever was at HOGWARTS.
It was the best evening of HARRY's life, better than winning at Quidditch, or Christmas, or knocking out mountain trolls... HARRY would never, ever forget tonight.
HARRY had almost forgotten that the exam results were still to come, but come they did. 
To their great surprise, both HARRY and RON passed with good marks; HERMIONE, of course, had the best grades of the first years. 
Even NEVILLE scraped through, NEVILLE's good Herbology mark making up for NEVILLE's abysmal Potions one. 
They had hoped that GOYLE, who was almost as stupid as NEVILLE was mean, might be thrown out, but NEVILLE had passed, too. 
It was a shame, but as RON said, you couldn't have everything in life.
And suddenly, their wardrobes were empty, their trunks were packed, NEVILLE's toad was found lurking in a corner of the toilets; notes were handed out to all students, warning them not to use magic over the holidays -LRB-``I always hope they'll forget to give us these,'' said FRED sadly-RRB-; HAGRID was there to take them down to the fleet of boats that sailed across the lake; they were boarding the HOGWARTS EXPRESS ; talking and laughing as the countryside became greener and tidier; eating BOTT's Every Flavor Beans as they sped past Muggle towns; pulling off their wizard robes and putting on jackets and coats; pulling into platform nine and three-quarters at King's Cross Station.
It took quite a while for them all to get off the platform. 
A wizened old guard was up by the ticket barrier, letting them go through the gate in twos and threes so they didn't attract attention by all bursting out of a solid wall at once and alarming the Muggles.
